#   15- 17 I3     ---          Num       Number of fitted epoches
#   19- 22 I4     mJy          <S>       Mean flux density at 15 GHz
#   24- 28 F5.2   mas          <R>       Mean distance (3)
#   30- 35 F6.2   pc           <dproj>   ? Mean projected distance (3)
#   37- 41 F5.1   deg          <theta>   Mean position angle (4)
#   43- 48 F6.2   deg          phi       Position angle of velocity vector 
#   50- 55 F6.2   deg        e_phi       Uncertainty in phi
#   57- 58 A2     ---        f_phi       Flag on phi (5)
#   60- 65 F6.2   deg          Diff      Offst between <theta> and phi
#   67- 72 F6.2   deg        e_Diff      Uncertainty in Diff
#   74- 75 A2     ---        f_Diff      Flag on Diff (6)
#   77- 83 F7.2   uarcsec/yr   pm        Proper motion
#   85- 90 F6.2   uarcsec/yr e_pm        Uncertainty in pm
#       92 A1     ---        f_pm        Flag on pm (7)
#   94-101 F8.5   ---          beta-app  ? Apparent speed in unit of c
#  103-110 F8.5   ---        e_beta-app  ? Uncertainty in beta-app
#  112-119 F8.3   yr           tej       ? Estimated epoch of origin
#  121-126 F6.3   yr         e_tej       ? Uncertainty in tej
#  128-134 F7.2   yr           tmid      Date of reference (middle) epoch
#                                         used for fit
#  136-143 F8.1   uarcsec      alpha-m   Fitted RA position (8)
#  145-149 F5.1   uarcsec    e_alpha-m   Uncertainty in alpha-m

# Note (2):
#     a = Individual feature epoch not used in kinematic fits.

# Note (5): A question mark indicates a feature whose motion is not consistent
#           with outward, radial motion but for which the possibility of inward
#           motion and its degree of non-radialness are uncertain.
#     c = Feature has significant inward motion according to the
#         vector motion fit.
# Note (6): A question mark indicates a feature whose motion is not consistent
#           with outward, radial motion but for which the possibility of inward
#           motion and its degree of non-radialness are uncertain.
#     b = Feature has significant non-radial motion according to the

#           motion and its degree of non-radialness are uncertain.
#     d = Feature has slow pattern speed.
